## Angular

> Angular is a web framework that empowers developers to build fast, reliable applications that users love.

### Updating Angular

* ğŸŒ [Official website](angular.dev/update-guide) - Interactive guide to help you migrate from one version of Angular to another.  
* ğŸŒ [Official update reference](angular.dev/cli/update) - Use the CLI to update your project or try new Angular features by adding the `--next` flag.
* ğŸŒ [Official migrations reference](angular.dev/reference/migrations) - Angular schematics help update projects by enabling conversion to standalone components, new control flow syntax, and more.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;159â­</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8ğŸ´</code></b> [ng-morph](https://github.com/taiga-family/ng-morph)) - Code mutations in your project or schematics were never easier than now.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;80â­</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;33ğŸ´</code></b> [ngx-libs](https://github.com/eneajaho/ngx-libs)) - Angular Libraries Support lists community libs support for each Angular version.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3â­</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0ğŸ´</code></b> [@fast-facts/ng-update](https://github.com/fast-facts/ng-update)) - A GitHub Action that keeps your Angular CLI-based projects up-to-date via automated PRs based on `ng update`.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2â­</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1ğŸ´</code></b> [npx-app-updater](https://github.com/DSI-HUG/ngx-app-updater)) - Alerts users to available updates when a new version is deployed.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3â­</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1ğŸ´</code></b> [ngx-update-app](https://github.com/Celtian/ngx-update-app)) - Angular directive for updating app via service workers.

## Architecture and Advanced Topics

### Feature Flags

* ğŸŒ [OpenFeature Angular SDK](openfeature.dev/docs/reference/technologies/client/web/angular) - A vendor-agnostic, community-driven API specification for feature flagging.
* ğŸŒ [@devcycle/openfeature-angular-provider](www.npmjs.com/package/@devcycle/openfeature-angular-provider) - ğŸŒ [DevCycle](docs.devcycle.com/sdk/client-side-sdks/angular/) supports the OpenFeature Angular SDK.
* ğŸŒ [@openfeature/go-feature-flag-web-provider](www.npmjs.com/package/@openfeature/go-feature-flag-web-provider) - ğŸŒ [GO Feature Flag](gofeatureflag.org/) provider allows you to ğŸŒ [connect](gofeatureflag.org/docs/sdk/client_providers/openfeature_angular) to your GO Feature Flag instance with the `@openfeature/web-sdk`.

### Accessibility

* ğŸŒ [Official Angular ARIA](angular.dev/guide/aria/overview) - A collection of headless, accessible directives that implement common WAI-ARIA patterns.
* ğŸŒ [digital.gov](digital.gov/guides/accessibility-for-teams/) - Accessibility for teams guide from USA government.
* ğŸŒ [WAI](www.w3.org/WAI/) - The W3C Web Accessibility Initiative (WAI) develops standards and support materials to help you understand and implement accessibility.
* ğŸŒ [webaim](webaim.org/) - Web accessibility in mind.
* ğŸŒ [WAVE](wave.webaim.org/) - Web Accessibility Evaluation Tools.
* ğŸŒ [axe Accessibility Linter](marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=deque-systems.vscode-axe-linter) - Accessibility linting for HTML, Angular, React, Markdown, Vue, and React Native.
* ğŸŒ [Angular Material CDK - a11y](material.angular.io/cdk/a11y/overview) - The a11y package provides a number of tools to improve accessibility.
* ğŸŒ [PrimeNG](primeng.org/guides/accessibility) - Accessibility guide from PrimeNG.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;28â­</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7ğŸ´</code></b> [astral-accessibility](https://github.com/verto-health/astral-accessibility)) - An open-source accessibility widget written in Angular.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2â­</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1ğŸ´</code></b> [angular-vlibras](https://github.com/angular-a11y/angular-vlibras)) - An Angular library that integrates VLibras to automatically translate content into Brazilian Sign Language (Libras).
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1â­</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0ğŸ´</code></b> [ngx-accessible-ui](https://github.com/ShakeelKadri/ngx-accessible-ui)) - Angular 9+ navigation and menu directives compliant with WCAG 2.1 AA and the European Accessibility Act 2025 for inclusive web experiences.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1â­</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0ğŸ´</code></b> [a11y-libraries](https://github.com/LDV2k3/a11y-libraries)) - A range of accessibility solutions for Angular.

### Security Best Practices

* ğŸŒ [Aikido](www.aikido.dev/) - Secure your code, cloud, and runtime in one central system. Find and fix vulnerabilities automatically.
* ğŸŒ [Angular Security](angular.dev/best-practices/security) - Best Practices.
* ğŸŒ [GitHub Code Scanning](docs.github.com/en/code-security/concepts/code-scanning) - Learn core concepts for GitHub's code scanning features.
* ğŸŒ [GitHub Skills](skills.github.com/) - Guided interactive tutorials for Code Security and analysis are available.
* ğŸŒ [HackTricks](book.hacktricks.xyz/network-services-pentesting/pentesting-web/angular) - Angular Security  Checklist.
* ğŸŒ [SafeDep](safedep.io/) - It continuously scans open source code for vulnerabilities and malware, helping security engineering teams proactively mitigate inherited OSS risks.
* ğŸŒ [Snyk](snyk.io/) - A developer security platform that integrates directly into development tools, workflows, and automation pipelines.
* ğŸŒ [Socket](socket.dev/) - A developer-first security platform that protects your code from both vulnerable and malicious dependencies.
* ğŸŒ [Vulert](vulert.com) - Secures software by detecting vulnerabilities in open-source dependenciesâ€”without accessing your code. It supports JS, PHP, Java, Python, and more.

### RxJS
